Count the frequency of each character in string t using a hash map 2. Initialize two pointers, l (left) and r (right), both at the start of string s 3. Use a hash map to keep track of the character counts in the current window of s 4. Expand the window by moving the right pointer r to the right, adding characters to the window 5. When the window contains all characters of t with the required frequencies (tracked by a variable formed), try to shrink the window from the left by moving l to the right, updating the minimum window size if a smaller valid window is found 6. If removing a character from the left causes the window to no longer satisfy the requirement, stop shrinking and continue expanding from the right 7. Repeat steps 4–6 until the right pointer reaches the end of s 8. Return the smallest window found that contains all characters of t, or an empty string if no such window exists |
